TOP TECHNICAL FAILURE RISKS AT 10 MILLION USERS
These are ranked by realistic danger level.

1 — Biggest Risk: Low-End Phone Performance
Why This Can Break Ecoskiller
Your target users:

Kids with ₹4,000–₹8,000 Android phones
Typical specs:

2–3GB RAM

Slow CPU

Weak GPU

If app becomes heavy:

Kids uninstall

Schools stop recommending

Growth stops

This is the #1 real-world failure risk.

Typical Failure Causes
Heavy UI
Bad:

Animations

Heavy images

Complex dashboards

Good:

Simple lists

Lightweight screens

Large App Size
Bad:

>100MB app
Good:

<25MB app
Critical.

Too Many Background Calls
Bad:

Good:

2 — Second Biggest Risk: Database Overload
At:

10 Million Kids
Expected:

Includes:

Missions

Rankings

Behavior logs

Ideas

System slows.

Then crashes.

Typical Failure Pattern

Read replicas

ClickHouse for logs

Critical.

3 — Third Biggest Risk: Leaderboard Calculations

Global rank

Class rank

Server dies.

Example Problem
10M users:

Millions of calculations per hour
Very heavy.

Prevention Strategy
Use:

Precomputed rankings

Every hour

Or every day

Not realtime.

At:

Impossible.

Failure Pattern
System becomes slow.

Idea submission freezes.

Stage 1:

Fast ML filtering
Stage 2:

AI comparison only on candidates

Example:

100,000 kids login in 1 hour
Servers crash.

Prevention Strategy
Must use:

Auto-scaling infrastructure
Mandatory.

Use:

Recommendations

10M users:

Huge data.

Days to finish

You said:
how to integrate coaching centres with ecoskiller, pros & cons

ChatGPT said:
Integrating coaching centres with Ecoskiller + SkillQuest + SchoolOS can become a major growth and revenue engine — but only if done carefully. Coaching centres are powerful partners because they bring students, teachers, and parents, but they can also create conflicts with schools if not positioned correctly.

Below is a complete integration strategy with pros & cons and the safest model.

1 — WHY INTEGRATE COACHING CENTRES
Coaching centres already have:

Large student bases

Competitive culture

Parents willing to pay

Regular classes

Example:

One coaching centre = 100–500 students
1000 centres:

≈ 200k–400k students
Huge growth channel.

2 — CORE STRATEGY
Coaching centres must be positioned as:

Skill Development Partners
NOT:

School Competitors
Critical.

If schools think Ecoskiller supports coaching instead of schools:

Schools may reject Ecoskiller.

3 — COACHING CENTRE INTEGRATION MODEL

Includes:

Feature	Purpose

SkillQuest	Activities
GD	Discussions
